                    if (xhr.status === 200 && xhr.readyState === 4) {
                        window.initialLoadProducts.resolvedData = {
                            response: xhr.responseText,
                            availabilityCriteria: JSON.parse(criteria)
                        }
                        window.initialLoadProducts.notify()
                    }
                }
                xhr.send(criteria)
            }
            function getLocationAndLoadProducts() {
                if (true && false && navigator && navigator.permissions) {
                    navigator.permissions.query({ name: 'geolocation' }).then(function(r) {
                        if (r.state === 'granted') {
                            getUserCoordinates().then(function(coordinates) {
                                loadProducts(coordinates)
                            }).catch(function(err) {
                                throw new Error(err.message)
                            })
                        } else {
                            throw new Error('No coordinates were found')
                        }
                    }).catch(function() {
                        localStorage.setItem('userCoordinatesOnFirstLoad', '{}')
                        loadProducts()
                    })
                } else if (true && false && navigator && navigator.geolocation) {
                    var userCoordinatesOnFirstLoad = localStorage.getItem('userCoordinatesOnFirstLoad')
                    var parsedUserCoordinatesOnFirstLoad = userCoordinatesOnFirstLoad && JSON.parse(userCoordinatesOnFirstLoad)
                    var isUserCoordinatesOnFirstLoadExists = parsedUserCoordinatesOnFirstLoad && parsedUserCoordinatesOnFirstLoad.hasOwnProperty('Latitude') && parsedUserCoordinatesOnFirstLoad.hasOwnProperty('Longitude')
                    if (isUserCoordinatesOnFirstLoadExists) {
                        getUserCoordinates().then(function(coordinates) {
                            loadProducts(coordinates)
                        }).catch(function() {
                            localStorage.setItem('userCoordinatesOnFirstLoad', '{}')
                            loadProducts()
                        })
                    } else {
                        localStorage.setItem('userCoordinatesOnFirstLoad', '{}')
                        loadProducts()
                    }
                } else {
                    loadProducts()
                }
            }
            getLocationAndLoadProducts()
        }
        </script>
